# KikiJarvis CRM — Session Handover (for the Kiki-Zentrale build)

> Paste this as starting context. Read `HANDOVER.md` for full detail. Scannable summary below.

## Recent changes
_Append one dated bullet per shipped, UI-visible change. Newest first._

- **2026-06-26 (branch `claude/happy-cray-201a0a`, pushed — NOT merged/deployed) — History-import follow-ups: auto-continue past the cap + progress shown in the Migration view.** Completes the two deferreds from the large-agent import fix. (1) **Auto-continue**: new `import_agent_history_until_done` ([history_import.py](backend/app/services/history_import.py)) loops `import_agent_history` until a pass reports `more=False` (or a `_MAX_PASSES=20` guard → "incomplete"), so a big back-catalogue finishes in one BackgroundTask without a manual re-trigger; each pass skips already-imported convs (idempotent, resumable). Both triggers (create-org + `POST /orgs/{id}/import-history`) now call it. (2) **Progress**: it records `{status, started_at, finished_at, imported, seen, errors, more, passes}` on additive `organizations.history_import_state` jsonb (migration `0081`, applied to UAT); `GET /orgs/{id}/migration` returns it and the **Migration view** ([AdminMigrationPage.tsx](frontend/src/admin/AdminMigrationPage.tsx)) shows an **"Import läuft… / abgeschlossen / N von M"** badge (amber spinner / green / red), polling every 4 s while running, with a >30-min "evtl. unterbrochen" staleness hint. Verified: real `_set_import_state` round-trip on UAT (kiki-test-007, then cleared); 27 touched-suite tests pass (incl. auto-continue + max-passes guard); tsc + build clean.

- **2026-06-26 (branch `claude/happy-cray-201a0a`, pushed — NOT merged/deployed) — Fix: customer-id (heykiki_org_id) is now server-generated, not hand-typed.** Amber: manual entry caused id clashes/typos — UAT data confirmed it (`kiki-customer-007`, `Kiki-customer-1009`, **`kiki-cutomer-0023`** [literal typo], `kiki-accept-vennemann`, `kiki-test-007`; prod uses `Kiki-Kunde-NNN`). The super-admin create form's `heykiki_org_id *` input is **removed** (replaced by a "wird automatisch vergeben" hint); the generated id shows on the success screen. New `next_heykiki_org_id(client)` ([provisioning.py](backend/app/services/provisioning.py)) scans existing ids **case-insensitively** for the highest `Kiki-Kunde-NNN` suffix and returns the next, zero-padded to 3 digits (format **chosen by Amber = `Kiki-Kunde-001`**); the `heykiki_org_id text unique` constraint backstops a concurrent-create race. `ProvisionRequest.heykiki_org_id` is now optional — omitted → auto-generated; an explicit value (n8n `/provision`) is still honoured + dup-checked. Note: UAT has no `Kiki-Kunde-*` rows yet, so the first UAT auto-create will be `Kiki-Kunde-001`; prod continues from its highest. 4 hermetic id tests + 40 touched-suite tests pass; tsc + build clean. No DB migration.

- **2026-06-26 (branch `claude/happy-cray-201a0a`, pushed — NOT merged/deployed) — Fix: historical call-import broke on large agents (~500–600 calls); now resilient + resumable + background-only.** Amber repro: creating an org for an existing customer worked at 31 calls but threw an "internal error" at ~600. Root causes in [history_import.py](backend/app/services/history_import.py): (1) the manual re-sync endpoint `POST /api/super-admin/orgs/{id}/import-history` ran the import **synchronously** → a multi-minute pull on a big back-catalogue timed the HTTP request out; (2) **no rate-limit/timeout backoff** → a rapid burst of hundreds of EL fetches gets throttled/errors; (3) re-runs **re-fetched everything** (dedup only ran post-fetch). Fixes: the manual endpoint now **schedules a BackgroundTask + returns 202** immediately (create path was already backgrounded); `_get_with_retry` adds exponential backoff on 429/5xx/timeout; `_existing_conversation_ids` bulk-preloads already-imported ids so re-runs **skip without re-fetching** (cheap + resumable after an interrupted pass); the whole run is defensive (one bad conv / mid-stream outage never aborts the batch or escapes the task); a **per-run cap of 1000** bounds a single pass (returns `more=True` → re-trigger to continue; 600 fits in one run). Idempotent via the existing-id skip + P0.2 dedup. 6 history-import tests updated/added (skip-without-fetch, cap→more, retry-stops-cleanly) — 20 touched-suite tests pass; route re-registers (202). **No DB migration, no UI change.** Follow-ups (not done): surface import progress in the Migration view + auto-continue past the 1000-cap.

- **2026-06-26 (branch `claude/happy-cray-201a0a`, pushed — NOT merged/deployed) — Kiki-Zentrale: "Anweisungen für Kiki" custom-instructions field + greeting cleanup.** Verhalten section: new ChatGPT/Claude-style free-text **"Anweisungen für Kiki"** with a rotating example placeholder (cycles domain hints while empty), stored on additive `agent_configs.custom_instructions` (migration `0080`, applied to UAT), rendered as a sanitized + length-capped `# Besondere Hinweise` block (`{{KZ_CUSTOM_INSTRUCTIONS}}`; sanitizer strips `{{tokens}}`/headers, caps length, empty→no section). Removed the **dead** "Begrüßungstext (von HeyKiki vorgegeben)" card (`welcome_message` singular was rendered nowhere + unread by the webhook), relabelled "Begrüßung" → "Begrüßung — was Kiki zu Beginn sagt", clarified the time-based card overrides it. 7 hermetic tests incl. a render-token integration check; tsc + build clean. No live render (offered).

- **2026-06-26 (branch `claude/happy-cray-201a0a`, pushed to origin — NOT merged/deployed) — Super-admin: phone required + auto-synced; + internal Migration view.** From Amber's "Custom Prompt Classification.xlsx" session (4 asks). **#1/#2 phone** ([AdminOrgFormPage.tsx](frontend/src/admin/AdminOrgFormPage.tsx)): the create form had **no** phone field → orgs created phoneless; now a **required "Telefonnummer"** + **"Aus ElevenLabs holen"** button that auto-fills the inbound HeyKiki number from the entered Sprach-ID. Root cause of "editing didn't clear the phone problem": `organizations.phone_number` is the **HeyKiki inbound number** (the agent's bound EL number = source of truth, also the KZ non-editable display + prompt contact), but `phone_bound` health checked **live EL only** and the edit never invalidated `['admin','agent-health']` (60s stale). Now `phone_bound` passes on **live EL OR stored org number**; new `lookup_inbound_number`/`sync_inbound_number` + endpoints `POST /lookup-agent-phone`, `POST /orgs/{id}/sync-phone`; edit-save invalidates the health board. **#3/#4 Migration view** ([AdminMigrationPage.tsx](frontend/src/admin/AdminMigrationPage.tsx), super-admin-only, route `/admin/orgs/:id/migration`, "Migration" action in the org list): **read-only** — (1) migrated-data counts (calls/customers/Anfragen/Vorgänge/Termine + last call); (2) prompt-divergence ([prompt_diff.py](backend/app/services/prompt_diff.py)) classifying the LIVE EL prompt vs the CRM's current template → Deckung %, INDIVIDUELL/STANDARDNAH, customer's own lines vs missing standard lines. **Nothing is ported** (Amber: "don't lay down the migration" yet); #4 strategy decided = route customer deltas into **Kiki-Zentrale config** (no prompt bloat), WerkPilot dropped. ⚠️ in-product Deckung % diffs vs the **current** template, NOT the Excel's old reference, so numbers won't match the spreadsheet (by design). Verified: classifier run live against real HSN agent → correctly CUSTOM; **70** affected backend tests pass; frontend `tsc -b` + build clean. **No live admin render** (super-admin Supabase session can't be minted). **No DB migration.**
- **2026-06-26 (merged to `main` on BOTH repos @ `8e5d978` — DEPLOYED to UAT via `railway up . --path-as-root --service frontend` AND to prod via `company/main` git-auto-deploy; both live-verified: `frontend-production-4bdf` + `crm.kikichat.de` PosteingangPage chunks carry "Transkript & Aufnahme"/"Nächste Schritte"/"Vorgang öffnen") — Made the Posteingang a real, informative inbox with INLINE-EXPANDING cards (accordion, NOT a drawer) + linked the dashboard deck into it.** Three asks: (1) **inbox cards summarize the case** instead of a one-line header — each shows customer + action title, a **cleaned summary of what's going on** (from the originating call's `data_collection.issue_summary`/`ultimate_summary` — already in the `/api/calls` list, **no extra fetch**; markdown flattened via `cleanText`) + the agent's **Nächste Aufgabe** (`next_action`). (2) **The Vorgang chip is clickable** → `/cases?case=<id>` (case) or `/vorgang/<inquiryId>` (thread); case/summary/next-action resolved from the action's OWN `call_id` (via a `callsById` map in `usePosteingang`) with inquiry-meta fallback — fixes data that was missing when the appointment's inquiry ≠ the call's. (3) **Info shows in place, not a drawer** (Amber: no side drawer/slider/extra component). The **summary** and **next steps** are ALWAYS visible as two **separate divided panels** — a `var(--ai-bg)` **ZUSAMMENFASSUNG** box (mirrors the call-detail summary box for consistency) + a `var(--surface-alt)` **NÄCHSTE SCHRITTE** box. Only the **transcript is behind its own toggle** ("Transkript & Aufnahme", collapsed by default) → expands inline to the call facts + transcript bubbles + recording (new [CallDetailInline.tsx](frontend/src/pages/posteingang/CallDetailInline.tsx), passed `showSummary={false}` so it doesn't duplicate the panel; **lazy-mounted on toggle**). Single-open per `expandedKey`; only cards with a `callId` get the toggle. The **employee-assign control (ZUSTÄNDIG) stays** (Amber likes it). **The ActionDrawer was deleted** (`ActionDrawer.tsx` removed from both pages). **Dashboard deck card → inbox:** clicking a card (or "Details →") navigates to `/posteingang?focus=<action_key>`; the inbox **scrolls to + green-ring-highlights** that card (summary/next-steps already visible; transcript stays collapsed — not auto-opened), then strips the param. The deck keeps quick appointment buttons + notify "prüfen" deep-links; its own drawer is gone. [api.ts](frontend/src/pages/posteingang/api.ts): `RawCall.data_collection`; `DecisionVM` gained `caseId`/`contextSummary`/`nextAction`; `buildDecisions(…, callsById)`. [PosteingangPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/PosteingangPage.tsx): accordion `DecisionCard` (`expanded`/`onToggle`/`onNavigate`/`highlighted`) + `?focus` effect + `openCase`. [DashboardPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/DashboardPage.tsx): `goToInbox`. **No backend change, no migration.** `tsc -b` green; no console errors. **Live-verified** (`localhost:5173`, `govindyadav0703@gmail.com`): Govind card shows the ZUSAMMENFASSUNG + NÄCHSTE SCHRITTE panels + the ZUSTÄNDIG assign; transcript hidden by default, opens on its toggle (facts + bubbles + recording, no duplicated summary), collapses again; clickable Vorgang chip → `/cases?case=…` opened "Floor Repair Appointment · VG-TD1009-0005"; dashboard card → inbox highlight (transcript stays collapsed). **Preview gotcha:** `launch.json` `cwd` must be **relative** to the worktree root (`"frontend"`), not absolute, or preview_start errors `cwd must be a relative path within the project root`.

- **2026-06-26 (branch `claude/objective-bouman-4c1a7d` @ `943995b`, DEPLOYED to UAT frontend `railway up --service frontend`; prod NOT done) — Made the dashboard "Jetzt entscheiden" decision deck (the `Alles erledigt 🎉` hero) functional AND split the cards into actionable vs notification by intent.** Two parts. **(A) Functional drawer:** new [ActionDrawer.tsx](frontend/src/pages/posteingang/ActionDrawer.tsx) — a right-side "open action" drawer (same shell/pattern as `CallDrawer`) showing the decision header + **proposed appointment slot** (new `dueAt`, Berlin-time), the **Vorgang** chip, **Kiki empfiehlt**, an inline **Zuständig** assign control, and — when the action resolves a `call_id` — the originating call's **Kiki-Zusammenfassung · Nächste Aufgabe · Transkript · Aufnahme-Player** (via the existing `useCallDetail`). [api.ts](frontend/src/pages/posteingang/api.ts): `DecisionVM` gained `callId` + `dueAt` (the backend `/api/actions/pending` already returned both; the VM was dropping them). HeroDeck does **optimistic removal** (`resolvedKeys`) so a resolved card vanishes instantly (no 30 s wait). **(B) Intent split (Amber's rule): ONLY appointment kinds are actionable; KVA/Rechnung + Rückruf are NOTIFICATION-only — no in-card business decision.** New `KIND_CFG` fields `notify` / `opensDrawer` / `cardCta` drive it: **appointment** kinds (`termin_anfrage`, `alt_time_proposal`, `appointment_cancelled`, `reschedule_unmatched`) keep the decision drawer (Bestätigen/Verschieben/Ablehnen + assign-before-confirm gating); **KVA/Rechnung with an existing document** (`kva_to_send`, `kva_pending_acceptance`, `invoice_to_send`, `invoice_pending_payment`) show a single **"Angebot/Rechnung prüfen →"** that deep-links to `/cost-estimates/:id` or `/invoices/:id` (decision happens in the doc's own page); **KVA/Rechnung suggested, no doc yet** (`kva_suggested`, `invoice_suggested`) open the **call-transcript drawer** whose onward action navigates to the pre-filled create-form; **`callback_owed`** is notification-only → **"Anrufer ansehen →"** to `/customers/:id` (was actionable Erledigt/Zuweisen — removed). The old one-click document decisions (send Angebot / accept-reject KVA / send invoice / mark-paid) are **gone from the deck** — `runResolve` now only POSTs for the 4 appointment kinds. [DashboardPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/DashboardPage.tsx) + [PosteingangPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/PosteingangPage.tsx): card subject/footer branch on `d.notify` (single "prüfen/ansehen" link vs decision buttons + "Details →"); shared `handleOpen` routes drawer-vs-navigate. **No backend change, no migration.** `tsc -b` green; no console errors. **Live-verified** (`localhost:5173`, `govindyadav0703@gmail.com` / TobiasDachdecker, 8 real pending decisions): Storno + Termin cards keep decision buttons + actionable drawer (Bestätigen + transcript + summary + slot "Mo., 29. Juni 11:00", assign-gated); a `kva_to_send` card shows only "Angebot prüfen →" and deep-links to `/cost-estimates/e320…`. ⚠️ Note: the **local UAT backend (port 8000) emits newer action kinds** — `appointment_confirmed`, `kva_accepted`, `kva_closed`, `invoice_cancelled`, `reschedule_pending` (from the unmerged `feat/scheduling-copilot-vacation-overhaul` branch) — which `KIND_CFG` doesn't know and silently filters out; on real `main` those aren't emitted, but if that branch merges, add their configs (and decide their notify/actionable intent) or they won't surface.

- **2026-06-25 (branch `claude/admiring-satoshi-125e6c` → `main`, DEPLOYED: prod via `company/main` auto-deploy + Railway UAT `railway up`) — Fix: Gesprächslogik (IF/THEN) changes never reached the ElevenLabs prompt.** Root cause was NOT the placeholder (verified `{{KZ_CONVERSATION_LOGIC}}` substitutes correctly with no leftover tokens, and `compile_conversation_logic` injects the "## Schritt 1a" block when enabled) — it was two silent gates: **(1)** `prompt_manual_override=True` made `rerender_and_push_for_org` no-op while `_repush_bg` reported it as a green "applied" success, so every config-driven push (IF/THEN, Leitfaden, …) silently never reached the agent while only the greeting (pushed via the separate `_el_patch` path in `/verhalten`) kept updating; **(2)** `conversation_logic_enabled=False` (rules saved but toggle off → correctly excluded, but invisibly). **Fixes:** [kiki_zentrale.py](backend/app/api/routes/kiki_zentrale.py) `_repush_bg` no longer treats `manual_override` as success → resolves the sync banner as failed w/ the `manual_override` sentinel; `GET /conversation-logic` defaults the toggle **OFF only for fresh orgs** (NULL `conversation_logic`), existing configured orgs keep their saved flag (no migration). [AgentSyncBanner.tsx](frontend/src/components/kiki/AgentSyncBanner.tsx): new amber "Gespeichert, aber nicht an Kiki übertragen" warning with a shared **`ForceResyncButton`** (force-resync + confirm, reused by the drift banner). [GespraechslogikSection.tsx](frontend/src/components/kiki/GespraechslogikSection.tsx): toggle defaults OFF; the editor (AI-generate + Wenn/Dann rules) **collapses when off** (toggle + Save bar + preview stay visible); **honest preview** — when off, the "So liest Kiki" preview sends empty rules so it shows only the Standard-Ablauf, exactly what the prompt receives. `tsc -b` green; backend **79** touched-suite tests pass (2 new `_repush_bg` tests). **Live UAT-verified** (kikitest01@gmail.com, org "Kiki Chat GmbH" — which had 2 rules saved but the toggle OFF, a real repro): collapse/expand, honest preview (1147→1454 chars on toggle), and a server-side `render_prompt_for_org` showing the IF/THEN block injected + zero leftover tokens. **No DB migration.** The `manual_override` warning banner itself was unit-tested only (no org in manual-override state on hand to live-render). **For an affected org:** check `GET /api/kiki-zentrale/drift` (`manual_override`) and the toggle; resync or enable accordingly.

- **2026-06-12 (branch `improvements-kiki-zentral` = `main`, LOCAL/UAT, NOT deployed) — HYGIENE BATCH: the 5 deferred audit items resolved.** **(1) stale-push race** — `rerender_and_push_for_org` now takes `expected_seq`, serializes the render→PATCH per org (process-local lock), and **skips with reason `superseded`** if a newer save's `agent_sync_seq` exists → overlapping saves are last-write-wins on the AGENT, not just the banner ([agent_config.py](backend/app/services/agent_config.py); `_repush_bg` passes the seq and treats `superseded` as a benign no-op). **(2) expiry-sweep starvation** — `run_due_reschedule_expiry` now scopes its query to **L3 orgs only** (`_l3_org_ids`) + `.order("reschedule_expires_at")`, so L1/L2 rows (never mutated; UI reads the column directly) can't crowd out due L3 rows in the `limit(200)`. - **2026-06-10 (branch `fix/reported-bugs-magiclink-confirm-dupphone`, LOCAL/UAT, NOT deployed) — bug #3 reschedule-duplicate fixed (admin-gated proposal + safety timer).** A reschedule never creates a second appointment: the agent (`change_appointment`) stamps the customer's requested slot onto the EXISTING row (`customer_proposed_*`) — no new row, no call/email sent — and the admin commits it (`approve-proposal` = in-place move + confirmation; `decline-proposal` = clear, and if the customer abandoned the old slot it cancels + notifies). New: agent asks the date when the customer has several upcoming appointments (precise link); captures `replace_original` intent; a per-org safety timer (`agent_configs.reschedule_request_timeout_hours`, default 24, set in Kiki-Zentrale → Autonomie → Termine) bounds the pending request. **Timer action is gated by appointments autonomy level** (reuses `appointments_level`): L1/L2 → only flag overdue in the UI (never auto-cancel a real booking); L3 → auto-resolve (drop the proposal; if replace-intent, cancel the slot + notify). Timer runs in the existing outbound sweep (`run_due_reschedule_expiry` in `outbound_dispatch`, best-effort so it can't break the reminder sweep) — no new infra. Migration **0063** (additive: `reschedule_expires_at`, `reschedule_replace_intent` on appointments; `reschedule_request_timeout_hours` on agent_configs) applied to prod DB. Reschedule approval modal now shows **old → new** + an "überfällig" flag. Removal is always `cancelled` (reversible), never hard delete. Verified: migration columns in DB, `tsc -b` clean, 18 appointment-route tests (incl. new decline-replace-intent test), Kiki-Zentrale timer input render-proven (L2 shows "überfällig markiert", L3 shows "automatisch aufgelöst"). ⚠️ Backend can't force the voice agent to pick "reschedule" over "new booking" — that's the ElevenLabs agent prompt/tool wording (small separate item); the backend now guarantees no duplicate row once a reschedule is recorded as a proposal.

  - **Leitfaden (item 12):** Pflichtfelder → **Leitfaden** (slug redirect): per-row on/off toggles, optional E-Mail field (opt-in), three VERKNÜPFT offer rows (Termin/KVA/Preisauskunft) two-way-synced with Autonomie/Preisauskunft (migration 0060); drag+toggles are local state with ONE batch save (`PATCH /leitfaden`) = ONE agent push; prompt renders the unified ordered guide.

- **2026-06-09 (🚀 DEPLOYED to prod — `main` `22a5e89`) — fixed the spiky `/api/customers?limit=500` 500s. Backend `d4165668` SUCCESS.** Root cause: the shared sync Supabase client fans out concurrent `run_in_threadpool` queries over ONE HTTP/2 connection → `httpx.RemoteProtocolError: ConnectionTerminated` (intermittent, hits every fan-out page). Fix: forced PostgREST to **HTTP/1.1** (connection pool, one conn per concurrent request) in `db/supabase_client.py`. Verified 40/40 concurrent → 200 on prod. (The earlier CORS-on-error fix just made this previously CORS-masked 500 visible.) Also backfilled `cancelled_at` for the test org's pre-fix cancellations so they surface as "Termin storniert" actions (user-approved).

- **2026-06-09 (🚀 DEPLOYED to prod — `main` `45314b8`) — ROOT-CAUSED + fixed the real "page crashes / cannot be reloaded" bug (it was NOT chunk-skew). Frontend deploy `159f8d5e` SUCCESS + backend `0133dcf2` SUCCESS (priors REMOVED; both verified via `deployment list`, not just CLI "complete"). Validated locally before deploy → no crash this time.**
  - **The crash = browser auto-translation.** `index.html` shipped `<html lang="en">` on a **German-only** app with no translate opt-out, so Chrome/Google Translate rewrote text nodes out from under React → `NotFoundError: Failed to execute 'insertBefore' on 'Node'` (the page break, on pages with NO code involvement — KVA form, cancelled-appointment route). Fix: `<html lang="de" translate="no">` + `<meta name="google" content="notranslate">`. ⚠️ **Side effect:** browser auto-translate is now disabled (correct — app is German-only by design; auto-translating crashed it). Verified live: prod serves `<html lang="de" translate="no">`.
  - **The intermittent CORS/500s were transient deploy-restart artifacts** (user tested seconds after a backend redeploy). Verified `/api/customers?limit=500` returns 200 **with** the `Access-Control-Allow-Origin` header. Hardened anyway: new http middleware (INNER to `CORSMiddleware`) returns a JSON 500 so unhandled errors flow back through CORS and carry the header — a bare Starlette `ServerErrorMiddleware` 500 lacks it, which is why a transient 500 showed as "blocked by CORS policy". +`test_cors_on_error`.
  - ⚠️ **The earlier "chunk-skew" hypothesis was wrong** — the `serve.json` no-cache/immutable headers are still a good practice (and live), but they were NOT the crash cause. The crash was translation. Don't re-attribute.

Verified the ACTUAL active deploys (not just CLI messages) + migration 0053 already applied to Supabase.**
  - ⚠️ **Frontend's FIRST deploy (`df0fbc61`) CRASHED → ~4 min prod 502** — `serve` (serve-handler) validates `serve.json` strictly and rejects unknown keys; my `$schema`/`comment` keys tripped `must NOT have additional properties` so `serve -s dist` wouldn't start. Hotfix `dc42136` stripped `serve.json` to the valid `headers`-only config; redeploy `65ea8290` SUCCESS. **Lesson reaffirmed:** always verify `railway deployment list` (CRASHED vs SUCCESS) — the `--ci` "Deploy complete"/exit-0 did NOT mean healthy. Also: `frontend/public/serve.json` must stay pure serve-handler config (no comments/$schema).

- **2026-06-08 (Architecture & performance hardening — from `ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-06-08.md`; branch `fix/arch-audit-hardening-2026-06-08`; LOCAL/UAT, NOT deployed) — fixes the correctness/security/leak findings from the multi-agent audit. Backend tests 536 pass / 6 PRE-EXISTING reds (unchanged baseline); frontend `tsc -b` clean; vitest 16 pass / 5 PRE-EXISTING reds (RufumleitungGuidePage).**
  - **P0 correctness / data-integrity (backend):** CSV-import dedup now PAGES past PostgREST's silent 1000-row cap (`csv_import.py` + `gen_customer_number`) — re-importing on an org >1000 customers no longer creates duplicates; same paging applied to the unbounded count/revenue/timeline reads (`customers._list` enrichment, `projects._list`, `dashboard._fetch_calls`/`_finanzen`, `build_customer_timeline`) so large orgs stop silently under-counting. Multi-write **atomicity**: `book_appointment` (inquiry→appointment) and `invoices._create` (invoice→KVA back-link) now compensate (delete the orphan) on a failed 2nd write. `post_call` L3 auto-confirm is now **idempotent** (conditional `update … where status='pending'` + gate notify on the returned row) → no duplicate real-customer confirmation calls/emails on overlapping webhook deliveries.
  - **P0 security:** removed the `master_webhook_secret="change-me"` fallback (now empty = fail-closed) + `validate_runtime_config()` aborts boot in `APP_ENV=production` when it (or DB creds) is unset; **FK-in-org** validation added to `projects._create` + `invoices._create` (service-role bypasses RLS → was an IDOR vector); JWKS cache TTL 1h→configurable 300s (`JWKS_TTL_SECONDS`).
  - **P1 parallelism / perf:** new `services/common.fetch_all_rows` (paging) + `run_parallel` (private threadpool — keeps the sync helpers sync so the direct-call unit tests stay green, no AnyIO starvation). Independent fan-out reads now run concurrently in `customers._detail`, `projects._list`, `employees._list`, `cost_estimates._list`, `dashboard._finanzen`, and both call timelines. `conversation_init` + `deps.get_current_user` no longer block the event loop (run_in_threadpool). `mark-read` 3 queries → 1 (common case). ElevenLabs tool-ID cache got a 1h TTL (was never re-fetched → stale ids forever). Outbound-dispatch occasion email is now 5s-bounded so a slow provider can't serialize the LIVE sweep. `calls` list `limit/offset` bounded.
  - **Frontend (UI-visible — responsiveness/leaks/padding):** Sidebar is now a **mobile drawer** (`md=768px`: backdrop + Escape + route-change close; static rail on desktop) with a Topbar hamburger; data tables (Kunden, KVAs) hide non-essential columns under `md`; Modal/Copilot-widget/profile-dropdown/CommandPalette sized to stay inside small viewports; overflow "leaks" fixed (`truncate`/`min-w-0` on call rows + workspace pane, Tag wraps on mobile); padding scale unified (Topbar/page/footer/hero). Re-render fixes: `useMemo` on Theme + AdminAuth context values. Leak fixes: shared `useToast` hook (effect-owned timer, replaces 7 uncleaned `setTimeout`s), idempotent OAuth-popup listener cleanup, `useMe()` de-dup. ⚠️ **Live preview render-proof at 375/768/1280 NOT yet done** (per the UI-done convention) — recommended before any prod deploy; Amber to verify manually.
  - **Deferred (documented in the audit, NOT bugs — too risky for a pre-prod window):** god-file → service-layer extraction; durable job queue for BackgroundTasks; full optimistic-update rollout; broad bare-except typing sweep. Tracked as P2/P3 in `ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-06-08.md`.

- **2026-06-05 (UAT — PERFORMANCE PASS: DB indexes + backend parallelism + frontend smoothness; LOCAL/UAT, NOT deployed) — from `PERFORMANCE_PLAN.md`, validated against the live DB (the CSV import already landed: ~4,880 customers across 5 orgs, so the slowness is present-tense, not hypothetical).**
  - **DB (applied to Supabase `ifbluvdcbcesuhvkxsfn`):** migration **0046** adds the 43 advisor-flagged FK covering indexes (`unindexed_foreign_keys` 43→0); **0047** drops the duplicate `idx_kva_org` + rewrites the `users_same_org` RLS policy to wrap `auth_org_id()`/`auth.uid()` in `(select …)` (init-plan; predicate/role/command unchanged → behavior-preserving).   - **Backend reliability (takes effect on uvicorn restart):** `dashboard.overview` was an `async def` calling the SYNC Supabase client directly → it blocked the event loop on ~8 serial HTTP calls, stalling the **whole worker** for every other concurrent user (the "falls over under load" cause the perf doc missed). Now offloaded + parallelized via `asyncio.gather(run_in_threadpool(...))` (non-blocking, ~1 round-trip). `customers._list` made async + parallelized (page query + 5 type-counts concurrent, then 3 enrichment counts concurrent) → ~11 serial round-trips → ~2 wall-clock; kept `count="exact"` (avoids PostgREST's 1000-row cap). A sweep confirmed dashboard was the ONLY blocking handler. `dashboard.py`, `customers.py`.
  - **Frontend smoothness:** optimistic call-delete (`onMutate` removes the row from `['calls']` instantly, rollback on error, reconcile on settle) — fixes the delete lag AND the "stuck on the transcript" race (auto-select now picks the correct next call from a list that no longer contains the deleted one); global React Query `staleTime: 30s` (no refetch-on-navigation); 21 route pages code-split via `React.lazy` + `Suspense` (smaller initial bundle / faster first paint). `CallDetail.tsx`, `main.tsx`, `App.tsx`.

"Kiki Chat GmbH"). Renamed the dict to `_WEEKDAY_ABBR_DE`. Prompt now renders (60k chars, no unfilled tokens). `agent_config.py`.

- **2026-05-28 — Agent-logic fix (backend, not UI): returning customers re-asked for their address.** On a repeat inbound call, `hk_identifyCustomer` returned `address: null` for an already-registered customer, so the agent (correctly, per prompt) re-collected the address. **Root cause:** `identify.py` carried a STALE private copy of `_format_address` that only parsed the `{street,city,postal_code}`/plain-string shapes — it had no `raw` branch, so it silently dropped every `{"raw": "..."}` address (the shape `get_or_create_customer`, `updateCustomerData`, and the CRM admin `_addr` all actually write). - **2026-05-28 — Wave 3 / Agent 3.2: unified `GET /api/calls/{id}/timeline` endpoint + vertical Verlauf-tab redesign (commit `bb00e5e`).** Replaces the customer-scoped Inquiries/Termine/KVA-accordion that the Verlauf tab used to render with a true call-scoped vertical timeline. **3.2.A — Backend** (`backend/app/api/routes/calls.py`): new `GET /api/calls/{id}/timeline` route + `_build_timeline(org_id, call_id)` helper. Aggregates 8 event kinds from existing columns — no new migration, no new `events` table. **Sources:** (1) `call_created` from `calls.started_at` (or `created_at` fallback); (2) `inquiry_status_changed` from `inquiries.updated_at` ONLY when `status != 'open'` (open = no transition yet, no event); (3) `appointment_confirmed` / `appointment_rejected` / `alternative_proposed` from `appointments.confirmed_at` / `rejected_at` / `alternative_proposed_at` (Wave 2.4's migration 0026 columns); (4) `kva_sent` / `kva_accepted` / `kva_rejected` from `cost_estimates.sent_at` / `accepted_at` / `rejected_at`. Each event carries `{id, kind, timestamp, actor_kind, actor_name, description, entity_id, extras}` — id is composed as `<entity>:<uuid>:<sub-event>` (e.g. `appointment:appt-1:confirmed`) so the React `key` is stable across re-renders. Actor inference is heuristic (no per-row "who changed it" audit column exists today): `call_created` → `actor_kind='kiki'`; `inquiry_status_changed` to in_progress/completed → `actor_kind='employee'`; appointment lifecycle events → `actor_kind='employee'`; KVA accept/reject → `actor_kind='system' actor_name='Kunde'` (the customer's decision); KVA sent → `actor_kind='employee'`. Sort: newest-first by ISO timestamp (`sort(key=lambda e: e['timestamp'], reverse=True)` — ISO strings sort lexicographically). **Tenant isolation:** every SELECT chains `.eq('org_id', org_id)`; cross-org call_id never matches the initial `calls` SELECT so `_build_timeline` returns `None` and the route translates to 404 before any aggregation runs (no info leak about other tenants' inquiry/appointment IDs). **assignment_changed event kind is reserved in the literal type but NOT surfaced in v1** — `inquiries.assigned_to` / `inquiries.assigned_employee_id` are overwritten in place with no audit row, so we'd have to invent history we don't have. Flagged as a follow-up that needs either an `agent_writes_audit`-style table for assignments OR widening the existing audit table's scope. **3.2.B — Frontend** (`frontend/src/pages/CallLogsPage.tsx`): `VerlaufTab({customerId})` becomes `VerlaufTab({callId})` — the prop type and the call site `{tab === 'course' && <VerlaufTab callId={call.id} />}` flip together. Inside, replaced the 3-section accordion (Durchgeführte Aktionen / Termine / KVAs) with a single vertical `<ol>` rendered inside a `relative pl-5` wrapper. **Visual:** 1px `bg-border` rail at `left-[7px]` running top to bottom; each event is an `<li className="relative">` with a 10px dot pinned at `-left-[18px]` (so it sits dead-centre on the 7px rail) with a 2px `ring-surface` ring so the dot reads cleanly above the rail. Each row has a meta row (relative time + actor chip) and a description line below. **Dot color map** (`TIMELINE_KIND_DOT`): call_created=blue-500 · inquiry_status_changed=muted · appointment_confirmed=green-primary · appointment_rejected=red-500 · alternative_proposed=amber-500 · kva_sent/accepted/rejected=purple-500/600/400 · assignment_changed=cyan-500 (reserved). **Actor chip** (`ACTOR_CHIP`): kiki=green-tint-50/green-deep · employee=blue-100/blue-800 · system=alt/faint — distinct visual lane per source so a scan groups "Kiki did X" rows apart from "Mitarbeiter did Y". **Relative-time formatter** (`relativeTimeDe`): "gerade eben" / "vor N Min" / "vor N Std" / "vor N Tagen" up to 7 days, then falls back to absolute short date (`28. Mai 2026`). Absolute timestamp on hover via `<time title={absoluteTimeDe(...)}>`. Empty state: simple `<p className="text-sm text-muted">Keine Verlaufs-Einträge.</p>` (no card frame). Loading state: "Lade Verlauf …". **Tab structure preserved** — the three tabs (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) and the tab bar UI are untouched; only the CONTENT inside `tab === 'course'` changed. **3.2.C — Code-tidy drive-by**: removed the now-unused `CustomerDetail` interface, `statusDot` helper, and `Euro` lucide import from the same file (they were only referenced by the old VerlaufTab body). Section / Tag / fmtTime / STATUS_TAG remain — still used by ActionsTab + DetailsTab. **Tests:** new `backend/tests/test_call_timeline.py` with **8 hermetic tests**: (1) cross-org call_id returns None (route → 404); (2) every per-table SELECT carries `.eq('org_id', ORG)` — recording `_FakeClient` asserts at least 4 org_id filters fire when inquiries/appointments/cost_estimates all have data; (3) `call_created` event always emitted, even on a brand-new call with no inquiries; (4) `status='open'` does NOT emit `inquiry_status_changed` (no transition has happened); (5) `status='completed'` emits the event with `actor_kind='employee'`, German label "Erledigt", extras carrying title + status; (6) all 3 appointment lifecycle events fire (confirmed / rejected with reason in extras / alternative_proposed); (7) all 3 KVA events fire with number flowing into extras, accept/reject get `actor_kind='system' actor_name='Kunde'`; (8) final list is strictly descending by ISO timestamp across all kinds, newest event (1h ago inquiry flip) at index 0, oldest (call_created 5 days ago) at the tail. Backend `pytest -q -m "not live"` = **137 passing, 6 deselected** (was 129; +8 mine; if Agent 3.1's mini-calendar +3 land separately, the total will roll up to 140). Frontend `npm run build` clean. **Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading + "Aufnahme laden" button untouched · clean centre conversation panel untouched · light Bot/User speaker icons untouched · three-tab right-panel structure (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) untouched · list-card enrichment (Wave 2.1) untouched · Anfragen/Aktionen tab switcher (Wave 2.2) untouched · right-panel polish (Wave 2.3) untouched · appointment card + mini-calendar slot (Wave 2.4 / 3.1) untouched. **Coordination with parallel Agent 3.1**: their `AppointmentCard.tsx` + `MiniCalendar.tsx` + `appointments.py` / `test_appointments_actions.py` work is in a different file set; my changes are confined to `calls.py` + the VerlaufTab function body + a new test file. No overlap, no merge conflict. **Deferred follow-ups:** (1) **`assignment_changed` event** — `inquiries.assigned_to` / `assigned_employee_id` is overwritten in place; the event kind exists in the TS literal type + the color-map but the backend never emits it. Surfacing this needs either (a) a new `inquiry_assignments_history` table written-to on every assign mutation, or (b) extending the existing `agent_writes_audit` scope to cover human assignments (currently agent-only). Either is its own change. (2) **Per-row "who changed it" actor names** — currently the actor for `inquiry_status_changed` and the appointment lifecycle events is the generic string "Mitarbeiter", because we don't store which specific user clicked the button. Adding `confirmed_by_user_id` / `rejected_by_user_id` columns to `appointments` (and similar for inquiries) would let us join through `users.full_name` and surface a real name. (3) **Realtime updates** — the timeline currently fetches once on tab open via TanStack `useQuery` with default staleness; if a sibling user confirms an appointment while this tab is open, the user has to switch tabs and back to see the new event. A Supabase Realtime channel on the relevant tables → cache invalidation would close that. (4) **Customer-name on KVA actor_name** — `kva_accepted` / `kva_rejected` currently say "Kunde" generically; resolving via the linked `customer_id` would let us say e.g. "Max Mustermann" instead. Minor enhancement. Per the local-UAT-Railway-prod-on-approval standing rule: committed + pushed to `origin/main`; **no `railway up`**. Backend uvicorn needs a manual restart to pick up the new `/api/calls/{id}/timeline` route (no `--reload`).

- **2026-05-28 — Wave 3 / Agent 3.1: compact 7-day mini-calendar inside `AppointmentCard` + new `/api/appointments/calendar` busy-slot endpoint.** Slots into the TODO marker left by Agent 2.4 (commit `9e7df01`) — replaces a HTML placeholder with a live 7-day grid that paints the proposed appointment + internal conflicts and lets the user click an empty cell to seed the Alternative-vorschlagen flow. **3.1.A — Backend `GET /api/appointments/calendar`** (`backend/app/api/routes/appointments.py`): new lightweight endpoint accepting `?from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD&self_id=...` and returning `[{id, start_time, end_time, status, is_self}, ...]`. Org-scoped via `require_org`; filters to `status IN ('pending', 'confirmed')` (cancelled/deleted aren't conflicts so they're dropped); derives `end_time` from `scheduled_at + duration_minutes` so the frontend doesn't have to recompute. `self_id` marks the currently-viewed appointment with `is_self=true` so the UI can render it as the highlighted green proposal rather than treating it as a conflict block. Deliberately kept separate from the existing heavier `GET /api/appointments` route (the latter pulls customer + employee join data the mini-calendar doesn't need, so paying that cost on every week shift would be wasteful). Re-used the appointments table's existing `org_id`/`scheduled_at` index pattern — no new migration needed. **3.1.B — New `MiniCalendar.tsx`** (`frontend/src/pages/calls/MiniCalendar.tsx`): standalone component, ~330 lines. Layout — 7 day columns (36px each, total 252px + 24px hour-label gutter = 276px wide, fits inside the 320px right panel with `p-2` padding) × 14 hour rows (20px each = 280px tall, 06:00-20:00 grid). Day-label row above the grid shows `Mo Di Mi Do Fr Sa So` + the date number; today's column gets a `bg-green-tint-50/40` wash + `text-green-primary` label. **3.1.B.1 — Coloring scheme**: proposed slot (the appointment being viewed, identified via `is_self=true` from backend OR via local `proposedStart`/`proposedEnd` props when not yet in the DB) = solid `bg-green-primary` block with white border and shadow. Internal conflicts colored by status: `status='confirmed'` = `bg-error/85` red block, `status='pending'` = `bg-warning/80` amber block. Blocks are absolute-positioned with `top = (start_hour - 6) * 20px` and `height = duration_minutes / 60 * 20px` (min 8px so a 15-min slot still has a visible bar). `pointer-events-none` on the blocks so the empty-cell click targets underneath still register. **3.1.B.2 — Click-to-propose**: every empty hour cell is a `<button>` covering the 20px row; clicking fires `onProposeSlot(start: Date, end: Date)` with a 1-hour range starting at the clicked hour. Past cells get `disabled` + `cursor-not-allowed` + `bg-alt/30` so the user can't propose a slot the backend would 422 anyway (the `/propose-alternative` route already validates `start_time > now()`, so this is a UX echo of the backend rule, not a duplicate of the auth check). **3.1.B.3 — Navigation**: `◀ ▶` lucide chevron buttons left/right of a centered window label (e.g. "28.–3. Jun" when same-month, "28.05 – 04.06" when crossing months). Each click shifts `weekStart` by ±7 days; TanStack Query refetches automatically because the window dates are in the `queryKey`. The window is anchored on the proposed slot's Monday if it's in a future week (so the user lands on the right week immediately), otherwise on today's Monday. **3.1.B.4 — Data fetching**: TanStack `useQuery` with `queryKey: ['mini-calendar', from, to, selfId]`, `staleTime: 60_000` (60s — matches the right-panel polling cadence; the mini-calendar doesn't need second-level freshness, the user-driven mutations on the parent card invalidate the cache when needed). `URLSearchParams` builds the query string so `selfId` is omitted cleanly when null. **3.1.B.5 — Legend**: 3 swatches below the grid (`Vorschlag` / `Bestätigt` / `Ausstehend`) at `text-[9px]` size — compact key so a new user can decode the color scheme without hunting through docs. **3.1.C — `AppointmentCard.tsx` integration**: replaced the `{/* TODO: Agent 3.1 mini-calendar — render <MiniCalendarSlot /> here once it's built. */}` comment marker (cleaned up the misnested `{/* {/*` typo on the same row while there) and added `<MiniCalendar>` between the alt-picker / lock-state UI and the action-buttons row — `!altAlreadySent && <MiniCalendar ... />` so the calendar disappears once the appointment is locked into "Alternative gesendet" state (the user can't propose new times then anyway). Added `proposedEndIso` memo computing `scheduled_at + duration_minutes` (fallback 60min) and a `handleMiniCalendarPick` callback that calls `setAltStart(dateToDtLocal(start))` + `setAltEnd(dateToDtLocal(end))` + `setAltPickerOpen(true)` — populates the existing date/time inputs and pops the picker open without auto-submitting (the user still clicks "Alternative senden" explicitly per spec). New `dateToDtLocal(d: Date)` helper extracted from the existing `isoToDtLocal` so both paths share the same `YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm` formatter. **3.1.D — Tests**: 3 new hermetic tests in `backend/tests/test_appointments_actions.py` (`test_calendar_busy_slots_returns_lightweight_shape` — pending + confirmed both surface, end_time = start + duration_minutes; `test_calendar_marks_self_id_correctly` — `self_id` matches stamp `is_self=true` on the right row and false elsewhere; `test_calendar_is_org_scoped` — recording `_FakeClient` confirms `.eq('org_id', user.org_id)` runs on the SELECT chain). Backend `pytest -q -m "not live"` = **140 passing, 6 deselected** (was 137 immediately before this commit; +3 mine in `test_appointments_actions.py` going from 12 → 15 tests — verified in isolation: `pytest tests/test_appointments_actions.py` → `15 passed`). Baseline rose well above the brief's expected 129 because Wave 2.2 (commit `96fadb3`, +8 tests) and Wave 3.2 (commit `5b45c6a`, +8 tests) both landed mid-Wave-3 between when the brief was written and when I shipped. Frontend `npm run build` clean (TS + Vite OK; pre-existing 1.7MB chunk-size warning is the unrelated app-wide concern that's been flagged in previous bullets — not introduced here). **Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading + "Aufnahme laden" untouched · clean centre conversation panel untouched · light Bot/User speaker icons untouched · three-tab right-panel structure (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) untouched · list-card enrichment untouched · Anfragen/Aktionen tab switcher untouched · right-panel polish (w-80, button compression, sticky-on-scroll) untouched · `AppointmentCard` header / Bestätigen / Ablehnen / Alternative vorschlagen / Ausblenden buttons all untouched in behavior — the calendar slots in between the picker and the buttons row, doesn't rearrange the existing surface. **Coordination with parallel Agent 3.2**: their Verlauf-tab work is in a different region of `CallLogsPage.tsx`; my changes are confined to `AppointmentCard.tsx` + the new `MiniCalendar.tsx` file. No overlap expected. **Deferred follow-ups**: (1) **External calendar sync (Google / Microsoft busy slots)** — the spec explicitly defers this to the OAuth bundle in a future session. Both the backend response shape (`{id, start_time, end_time, status, is_self}`) and the frontend rendering (color-by-status) are designed so an external-sync layer can merge `status='external'` blocks in without a schema change. TODO comment placed in `appointments.py` above `_calendar_busy_slots` and a corresponding note in `MiniCalendar.tsx`'s module docstring. (2) **Vertical zoom / non-1h granularity** — current grid is locked at 1-hour rows because the propose-alternative endpoint only accepts hour-aligned slot starts in practice. If 30-min granularity becomes a real ask, halve `HOUR_ROW_PX` (currently 20) and emit two `<button>` cells per hour. (3) **Drag-to-resize on proposed block** — the current click-to-propose always creates a 1-hour range; a drag affordance to set custom-duration ranges would be nicer UX but adds non-trivial pointer-event handling. (4) **Week label keyboard nav** — `◀ ▶` are mouse-clickable today; binding `←`/`→` arrow keys when the calendar has focus would help power users. (5) **Cross-day appointments** — the current renderer assumes every appointment fits inside a single day; an appointment that straddles midnight would only render its start-day portion. Not realistic for tradesperson appointments but worth flagging if the feature gets re-used elsewhere. - **2026-05-28 — Wave 2 / Agent 2.1: call/inquiry list-card enrichment — employee avatar, status pill, NOTDIENST badge, recent-unread glow, inline assign-employee dropdown (commits `cb31508` + `dc70e70`).** Backend half (`cb31508`): `/api/calls` list endpoint enrichment + new `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}/assign` route + migration 0024 + 12 hermetic tests. **2.1.A — Backend list endpoint** (`backend/app/api/routes/calls.py`): `_LIST_SELECT` gains `created_at`; new `_enrich_calls_with_inquiries` helper batch-fetches inquiries (filtered to `org_id` + `call_id in ...` + `status <> deleted`, ordered by `created_at ASC` so the earliest non-deleted inquiry per call wins on multiples) + the employees those inquiries reference (1 SELECT + 1 SELECT, no N+1). Surfaces 5 new fields per call row: `inquiry_id` (uuid | null), `inquiry_status` ('open' | 'in_progress' | 'completed' | null), `emergency_flag` (bool — true when `inquiries.emergency_flag` is true OR `inquiry.type ∈ {'notdienst', 'notfall', 'emergency'}` to catch legacy / AI-classified rows that stuffed the urgency into `type` instead of toggling the new column), `assigned_employee_id` (uuid | null), `assigned_employee_initials` (str ≤ 2 chars | null — first 2 chars for single-word names, else first + last initial, both uppercased). **2.1.B — Migration `0024_inquiry_emergency_flag.sql`** (additive, pre-authorized): `ALTER TABLE inquiries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS emergency_flag boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` + partial index `idx_inquiries_emergency_open ON inquiries (org_id) WHERE emergency_flag = true AND status <> 'deleted'` for fast urgent-only filtering. Applied via Supabase MCP; verified via `information_schema.columns` (boolean, NOT NULL, default false). `inquiries.assigned_employee_id` already existed (added in 0005). **2.1.C — `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}/assign`** (`backend/app/api/routes/inquiries.py`): body `{employee_id: uuid | null}`; auth-gated via existing `require_org`. Pre-checks that the inquiry belongs to the caller's org (404 if not — no info leak about other tenants' inquiry IDs). When `employee_id` is non-null, validates that the employee row exists, is `deleted=false`, AND has the same `org_id` (422 with German message "Mitarbeiter gehört nicht zu dieser Organisation." otherwise — explicit cross-org guard so a malicious org_admin can't reassign their inquiry to another tenant's employee even if they know the UUID). When `employee_id` is null, the employee-validation step is skipped entirely (so unassigning works cleanly without needing a non-existent employee to exist). Distinct route from the generic `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}` so the frontend can fire a focused mutation and test coverage doesn't conflate concerns. **Frontend half** (`dc70e70`, `frontend/src/pages/CallLogsPage.tsx`): 5 new visual elements on each list-item card in the LEFT sidebar, all enriching, none replacing existing layout. **2.1.D — Employee avatar** (24px): color-hashed by `assigned_employee_id` via a stable djb2-ish hash (`hash = (hash * 33 + charCode) >>> 0`) mapped to one of 6 pastel-saturated palettes (blue / amber / purple / pink / cyan / teal — order locked because reordering would visually reassign every employee in production). Same employee always renders in the same color across the list, page reloads, and sessions. Unassigned rows render `?` in a neutral `bg-alt text-faint` circle. **2.1.E — Status pill**: small chip in the meta row — `Offen` (blue-100/blue-800) · `In Bearbeitung` (amber-100/amber-800) · `Erledigt` (green-100/green-800). Null or 'deleted' status → no pill rendered at all (graceful absence). **2.1.F — NOTDIENST badge**: red `AlertTriangle` + "Notdienst" caps chip in the top-right corner when `emergency_flag=true`, absolute-positioned so it doesn't fight the right-aligned phone-direction icon for inline space. **2.1.G — Recent-unread glow**: `ring-2 ring-green-primary/40 animate-pulse` on cards where `read_at IS NULL` AND `created_at > now() - 1 hour`. The 1-hour window is intentional — without the time cap every unread card would pulse forever and the visual signal would lose all meaning. Glow ring sits under the active-state border so the selected-card highlight still wins visually when both apply. **2.1.H — Inline assign-employee dropdown**: clicking the avatar opens a Radix DropdownMenu listing every employee in the org (each with their own color-hashed mini-avatar), plus a top "— Niemand —" item to unassign. Selecting an item fires `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}/assign`; on success, invalidates both `['calls']` (refreshes the avatar) and `['callInquiry']` (keeps the right-panel Aktionen `<select>` in sync). Disabled when the call has no inquiry yet (German tooltip). **Structural change**: the card outer element switches from `<button>` to `<div role="button" tabIndex={0}>` because the nested DropdownMenu.Trigger `<button>` would be invalid HTML inside another button. Keyboard equivalents (Enter / Space → onSelect) preserved. Avatar click `e.stopPropagation()` so the avatar click doesn't ALSO fire the card-body onSelect. **Drive-by fix**: re-exported `ACTION_KIND_LABEL` (declared earlier by Agent 2.2's WIP) so `tsc --noUnusedLocals` stops failing the build during the brief window before their AktionenList renderer commits. Functionally a no-op; `export` just satisfies the linter. **Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading + "Aufnahme laden" button untouched · clean centre conversation panel untouched · light Bot/User speaker icons untouched · three-tab right-panel structure (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) untouched · bot-icon empty-bubble skip (`!hasMessage && visibleToolCalls.length === 0`) untouched. **Coordination with sibling agents**: separate file regions, no overlap. - **2026-05-28 — Wave 2 / Agent 2.2: Anfragen/Aktionen tab switcher above the call-list + `/api/actions/pending` aggregation route.** New tab strip above the LEFT-sidebar search bar of `CallLogsPage.tsx`: **Anfragen** (default, current list — Agent 2.1's surface, untouched) and **Aktionen** (new) with a red `bg-red-500` count badge `rounded-full text-[10px] px-1.5 text-white` showing total pending decisions (hidden when 0). Search bar is intentionally hidden on the Aktionen tab — searching aktionen wasn't in scope for v1 (spec allowed the simpler path); flagged as a follow-up. **2.2.A — Backend route** in new `backend/app/api/routes/actions.py`: `GET /api/actions/pending` returns a single `list[ActionItem]` aggregated from across the org's existing tables. Per-kind aggregators are isolated functions so each is independently testable/mockable: (1) **`termin_anfrage`**: `appointments.status='pending'` (the existing enum is `pending|confirmed|cancelled|completed` — there's no `pending_confirmation` value in current schema, so `pending` is the right "Kiki proposed, needs human confirm" bucket); (2) **`kva_to_send`**: `cost_estimates.status='draft' AND created_at <= now()-24h`; (3) **`kva_pending_acceptance`**: `cost_estimates.status='sent' AND sent_at >= now()-7d AND accepted_at IS NULL AND rejected_at IS NULL` (belt-and-braces filter — the enum constraint already drops accepted/rejected but a stale row could carry status='sent' + accepted_at, so we filter in Python too); (4) **`callback_owed`**: **EMPTY in v1** — `inquiries.status` enum is `open|in_progress|completed|deleted`; there is no `callback_required` value. Returns `[]`; documented in module docstring. (5) **`alt_time_proposal`**: **EMPTY in v1** — `appointments` had no `alternative_proposed_at` column at the time I designed this. Agent 2.4 added these columns in migration `0026` (committed `9e7df01`); my route still returns `[]` for this kind to keep aggregation deterministic across the migration boundary — a future commit can flip this on once the column is in live Supabase and we want the alternative-proposed flow showing in Aktionen. Sort: priority desc (high→normal), due_at asc nulls last, created_at desc; stable 3-pass sort (created_at first, then due_at presence + due_at value, then priority — Python's stable sort makes this clean). Each item: `{kind, id, inquiry_id, call_id, customer_name, customer_id, summary, created_at, due_at, priority}`. Auth-gated by `require_org` (org-scoped). Wired into `backend/app/main.py`. **2.2.B — Frontend wiring**: new `ActionItem` TS interface + `ACTION_KIND_LABEL` German chip-label map (`Terminbestätigung` / `KVA senden` / `KVA-Antwort offen` / `Rückruf` / `Alternativtermin`) live on the client so the wire format stays language-neutral. `actionsQuery` uses TanStack `useQuery` with `refetchInterval: 30_000` (matches the dashboard overview poll cadence — appointments/cost_estimates don't have a realtime channel today) + `staleTime: 10_000` so the badge stays visible across tab flips without flicker. **2.2.C — Aktionen tab content**: new `AktionenList` + `ActionListCard` components rendered when `tab === 'aktionen'`. Each card: small priority dot (red for `high`, green for `normal`), kind chip (info-bg/info-text), timestamp (due_at preferred, else created_at), bold summary line, customer name. Empty state: "Keine offenen Aktionen. — Kiki hat alles im Griff." (no card render, just centered text). **2.2.D — Click navigation**: v1 navigates to `/customers/{customer_id}` when the item carries one (existing route). The panel is already structurally pinned (flex sibling of the transcript column in a `flex h-full min-h-0` parent — each owns its own `flex-1 overflow-y-auto` content area, so the right panel doesn't scroll when the transcript does), so sticky is a no-op today; it kicks in only if a future restructure flips the parent to a vertical stack. Inline comment documents this so the next maintainer doesn't trip over it. **2.3.D — Zusammenfassung preview card at TOP of center panel:** new compact card directly below the transcript header, ABOVE the audio player, when `call.summary` is non-empty. Hidden entirely otherwise (no empty card render — `summary && (...)`). 2-line truncated body (`line-clamp-2`, already in use elsewhere in the codebase per Tailwind 3.3+ built-in) + Sparkles AI icon (visual lineage with the Details-tab Zusammenfassung Collapsible) + "Mehr anzeigen" link that calls a new `onOpenSummary` callback prop threaded down from `CallDetail` (new prop on `Transcript`) which calls `setTab('details')` on the right panel — opens the full summary in the existing Details-tab Collapsible without duplicating content. No backend changes needed. **Implementation:** new `useRef<HTMLAudioElement>` on the lazy-mounted `<audio>` element; `useEffect` wires `timeupdate` / `pause` / `ended` listeners that compute the active turn index via linear scan through a pre-sorted `timedTurns` memo. Highlights the active turn with a soft tint behind the whole row (`bg-green-tint-50` for Kiki / `bg-info-bg` for the customer — chosen so the existing bubble colors stay the focal point and the wash reads as a secondary halo) + `shadow-e1` on the bubble itself. `scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'nearest'})` keeps the highlighted turn visible without fighting the user's manual scroll. Returns to no-highlight (`activeIdx = -1`) on pause/end. **Graceful fallback:** when the transcript has zero timed turns (older imports), shows a `text-faint` "Älterer Anruf — Sprungmarken nicht verfügbar." hint next to the audio controls and skips the highlighting entirely. **Wins preserved:** lazy audio loading + "Aufnahme laden" button untouched (the listener attaches via `audioRef.current` once the element mounts — works seamlessly with the existing eager-load gate); three tabs (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) untouched; speaker icons (Bot / User) untouched; empty-bubble skip logic (`hasMessage && !visibleToolCalls.length` → `return null`) untouched. **Coordination with parallel agents:** Agent 2.4's `AppointmentCard` sits at the TOP of my `sticky w-80` aside (commit `9e7df01` landed first, my changes preserve the insertion slot); Agent 2.1's list-card enrichment (commit `cb31508`) is in the left aside which I didn't touch; Agent 2.2's left-tab switcher work is still in-flight in the working tree, didn't conflict with my CallDetail/Transcript edits. **Tests:** no new tests (UI-only change). Frontend `npm run build` clean (TS + Vite OK). Backend `pytest -q -m "not live"` = **117 passing, 6 deselected** (no regression from my changes; +20 added by Agents 2.1+2.4 in their commits). - **2026-05-28 — Wave 2 / Agent 2.4: inline OFFENE AKTIONEN appointment card on the call-detail right panel + 3 action routes.** New surface at the TOP of the right panel of `CallLogsPage.tsx` (above the title block / tabs), rendered conditionally when the selected call has a `status='pending'` appointment linked to its inquiry. **2.4.A — Backend routes** in `backend/app/api/routes/appointments.py`: (1) `POST /api/appointments/{id}/confirm` — flips status `pending`→`confirmed`, stamps `confirmed_at = now()`, clears any stale `alternative_proposed_at`. (2) `POST /api/appointments/{id}/reject` — body `{reason?: str}` — flips status `pending`→`cancelled` (re-uses the existing terminal status; the discriminator between a hard-reject and a customer-initiated cancel is `rejected_at IS NOT NULL`), stamps `rejected_at = now()` + optional `rejection_reason`. (3) `POST /api/appointments/{id}/propose-alternative` — body `{start_time: datetime, end_time: datetime, note?: str}` — fills `alternative_start_time` / `alternative_end_time` / `alternative_note` / `alternative_proposed_at`; status STAYS `pending` (card flips visually to "Alternative gesendet" by reading the timestamp, not the status). All three: tenant-scoped (`org_id` filter on SELECT before UPDATE → cross-org IDs return 404); state-machine guard (409 if status ≠ `pending`); `propose-alternative` adds `422` validation (start < end + start in future). Bonus sibling lookup route `GET /api/appointments/by-call/{call_id}/pending` returns `{appointment: AppointmentPreview | null}` so the frontend can decide whether to render the card (separate from `/api/calls/{id}` to avoid stepping on Agent 2.1's parallel calls.py changes; the keyed lookup walks `calls → inquiries (call_id=…) → appointments (inquiry_id=…, status='pending')`, picks earliest `scheduled_at` if multiple). **2.4.B — Migration `0026_appointment_alternative.sql`** (additive, pre-authorized) adds 7 nullable columns to `appointments` (`confirmed_at` / `rejected_at` / `rejection_reason` / `alternative_start_time` / `alternative_end_time` / `alternative_note` / `alternative_proposed_at`) + partial index `idx_appointments_pending_by_inquiry` on `(org_id, inquiry_id) WHERE status='pending'` for fast card-pending lookups. **No status check-constraint changes** — I initially planned to widen the enum with `pending_confirmation` / `rejected` / `alternative_proposed` statuses, but the classifier (correctly) flagged the DROP+ADD CHECK as non-additive, so I re-designed to encode the new lifecycle in timestamp + text columns and re-use the existing `pending|confirmed|cancelled|completed` enum. Reject re-uses `cancelled`; alternative-proposed stays `pending`. Cleaner anyway. **2.4.C — New `AppointmentCard.tsx`** under `frontend/src/pages/calls/`: matches the WerkPilot reference card pattern (`02-pending-appointment-card.png` / `03-appointment-expanded.png` / `04-employee-dropdown.png`) — date/time + location header, "Wartet auf Bestätigung" green pill (or "Alternative gesendet" info pill when locked), expandable "Kategorie, Dauer & Zuweisung" toggle that reveals: Kategorie dropdown (sourced from `/api/kiki-zentrale/appointment-categories`), Dauer pills (30/60/90/120 Min) + Benutzerdefiniert numeric input, Mitarbeiter dropdown (sourced from `/api/employees`). Category pick auto-fills duration + default_employee + shows "Defaults für '<category>' wurden übernommen — du kannst sie unten überschreiben." Action buttons row: **Bestätigen** (primary green) → `POST /confirm` · **Alternative vorschlagen** (lighter green-tint-200) → opens inline date/time picker → `POST /propose-alternative` · **Ablehnen** (bg-faint gray) → `POST /reject` · **Ausblenden** (border outline) → client-side dismiss via `Set<string>` of appointment ids in the parent component (no server write; per-session). Hooked into `CallLogsPage::CallDetail` with a `usePendingAppointment(callId)` TanStack Query hook (staleTime 60s, invalidated on every action). Card renders **above** the title block; tabs (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) and their contents are **untouched** (Agent 2.3's surface). **2.4.D — Mini-calendar slot reserved for Agent 3.1**: inside the card header row, an HTML comment marker `{/* TODO: Agent 3.1 mini-calendar — render <MiniCalendarSlot /> here once it's built. */}` plus a sibling render slot in the OFFENE AKTIONEN header. The card's outer wrapper has clean `space-y-3` between sections — Agent 3.1's 7-day mini-calendar can drop in either above the action buttons or beside the date/time header without restructure. **2.4.E — Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading, clean center transcript, light speaker icons, three right-panel tabs (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf), bot-icon-empty-bubble fix — all untouched. **Tests:** new `backend/tests/test_appointments_actions.py` with **12 hermetic tests** (3× confirm: happy path + 404 cross-tenant + 409 not-pending · 3× reject: happy path + no-reason ok + 409 not-pending · 3× propose-alternative: happy path keeps status='pending' + 422 start≥end + 422 past · 3× pending-for-call lookup: appointment present + no-inquiry returns null + 404 call missing). - **2026-05-28 — Wave 1 / Agent 1.2: 3-tier `send_email()` fallback chain (Gmail/MS OAuth → customer SMTP → Brevo).** P1.8 Phase 3 send refactor. NEW shared module `backend/app/services/email_send.py` exposes `send_email(*, org_id, to_email, subject, body_html, body_text, attachments, cc, bcc) -> SendResult` with `Attachment` dataclass + `ProviderUsed` literal (`gmail_oauth` / `ms_oauth` / `customer_smtp` / `brevo_smtp`). **Tier 1 (OAuth):** reads `email_configs.oauth_provider` + `oauth_refresh_token_encrypted` etc. (shipped by P1.8 Phase 2 / commit `8e6099b`); refreshes the access token via `POST {provider_token_url}` with `grant_type=refresh_token` when expired or within 60s of expiry, persists the new token back to `email_configs` (best-effort); sends via Gmail API `users/me/messages/send` (RFC 5322 MIME base64url-encoded) for Google, or `POST /v1.0/me/sendMail` (base64 file attachments) for Microsoft Graph. Provider 1/2 are mutually exclusive per org. **Tier 2 (customer SMTP):** reads `smtp_host`/`smtp_port`/`smtp_username`/`smtp_password_encrypted`/`smtp_sender_*`/`use_ssl` (existing P1.4 columns), decrypts via Fernet (`app.core.crypto`), opens `smtplib.SMTP_SSL` (use_ssl=True) or `smtplib.SMTP` + STARTTLS (with fallback if relay doesn't speak STARTTLS), authenticates, sends. **Tier 3 (Brevo fallback):** central HeyKiki relay via env vars `BREVO_SMTP_HOST` (default `smtp-relay.brevo.com`) / `BREVO_SMTP_PORT` (default `587`) / `BREVO_SMTP_USERNAME` / `BREVO_SMTP_PASSWORD` / `BREVO_SMTP_FROM_ADDRESS` (default `no-reply@heykiki.de`) / `BREVO_SMTP_FROM_NAME` (default `HeyKiki`). From-name renders as `"<org> via HeyKiki"` so recipients see the originating org. All 6 vars added to `backend/app/core/config.py` `Settings` class + `backend/.env.example` (placeholders only; `backend/.env` not touched per memory note). **Behavior:** every step logged (info on success, warning on tier failure, error on full failure); tier failures captured in `SendResult.fallback_chain` as `['gmail_oauth_failed','customer_smtp_failed','brevo_smtp_success']` (etc.); if every tier fails, raises `RuntimeError` with full chain summary so the caller knows. Attachments work cleanly across all 3 tiers (Gmail = base64url MIME blob; Graph = base64 fileAttachment array; SMTP = stdlib `add_attachment`). **Refactored call sites:** (a) `backend/app/api/routes/cost_estimates.py::send_estimate` — now renders the KVA/Angebot/AB PDF, builds subject+HTML body from customer-stored templates (`kva_email_subject`/`kva_email_body` from `email_configs`; supports `{number}`/`{customer_name}`/`{org_name}` substitution) or German default, calls `send_email`, **stamps `status='sent'` ONLY on success** (previously stamped before sending, leaving status incorrect on send failure), returns `{success, status, emailed: true, to, provider_used, fallback_chain}`. (b) `backend/app/api/routes/invoices.py::send_invoice` — same shape for invoice PDFs + `invoice_email_subject/body` templates. (c) `backend/app/api/routes/settings.py::email_test` — now uses the chain instead of inline `smtplib`; returns `{success, message, provider_used, fallback_chain}` so the admin can see which tier succeeded (useful for verifying a freshly-pasted SMTP config or OAuth link). Dropped the now-unused `smtplib`/`EmailMessage`/`decrypt` imports from settings.py. **No deps added** — used `httpx` (already pinned) for OAuth refresh + Gmail/Graph REST instead of pulling in `google-auth`+`googleapiclient`+`msal`. **Tests:** new `backend/tests/test_email_send_fallback.py` with **10 hermetic tests** mocking httpx + smtplib (Gmail OAuth happy path + no SMTP attempted · MS Graph 202 OAuth happy path · OAuth fails → customer SMTP succeeds · OAuth + customer SMTP fail → Brevo succeeds · all 3 fail raises with full chain · no config → straight to Brevo · SMTP-only config skips OAuth tier · expired access token triggers refresh + uses fresh token downstream · Brevo creds missing at last tier raises · MIME builder attaches PDF + Cc + html→text fallback). Backend `pytest -q -m "not live"` = **97 passing, 6 deselected** (was 87 after Agent 1.3; +10 new). Frontend `npm run build` clean (UI unaffected — this is a backend-internal refactor; the send buttons in the existing KVA/Rechnung detail pages now actually deliver email instead of just stamping `sent_at`). **Behavioral note for UAT:** until Amber pastes real `BREVO_SMTP_USERNAME` + `BREVO_SMTP_PASSWORD` into `backend/.env` (and Railway env vars for prod), the fallback tier will raise `"Brevo SMTP credentials not configured"` — orgs without OAuth + without customer SMTP can't send. The error message is explicit and surfaced in the 502 response body. **Deferred follow-ups:** (1) **Brevo account + credentials** — Amber needs to create the Brevo account (or reuse an existing one), grab the SMTP credentials from the dashboard, and paste them into both `backend/.env` (local UAT) and the Railway backend's env vars before any send-from-org-without-OAuth path can succeed. Until then the customer-portal `/send` button on KVA/Rechnung detail pages will only work for orgs that have either OAuth-linked Gmail/Outlook OR pre-existing SMTP. (2) **Frontend OAuth connect buttons + send-status surface** — the customer-portal Settings page needs Gmail/Microsoft "Verbinden" buttons that hit `GET /api/settings/oauth/{provider}/authorize` and open the popup. Separately, the KVA/Rechnung send success toast could show `provider_used` so customers can see which channel actually delivered. Out of Wave 1.2 scope; flagged for the next wave. (3) **Reply-To header per org** — currently emails sent via Brevo show envelope-from `no-reply@heykiki.de`; setting `Reply-To` to the customer's `org.email` would let replies route back. The MIME builder already accepts `reply_to_email`, just not wired up yet for the Brevo path. Per the local-UAT-Railway-prod-on-approval standing rule: committed + pushed to `origin/main`; **no `railway up`**. - **2026-05-27 — Step A: split Supabase auth clients + fix `/admin/orgs` 500.** Two bugs blocking UAT of the standalone super-admin surface. **Bug 1 (same-Chrome session collision):** customer portal and admin surface shared Supabase's default `sb-*-auth-token` localStorage key, so signing in on one kicked the other out. Postgrest returned `APIError: column organizations.updated_at does not exist` → the route raised a 500 → Chrome surfaced it as `net::ERR_FAILED` / "Failed to fetch" instead of an HTTP-error popup. Fix: migration `0021_org_updated_at` adds `organizations.updated_at timestamptz NULL` (additive, no backfill — new writes stamp via existing `_now()`; old rows render `—` until next PATCH); applied via Supabase MCP. After the migration both endpoints return 200 with the org list + stats. **Verification (in-browser via preview MCP, single Chrome tab):** (a) `/admin/login` as `amber@gmail.com` → land on `/admin/orgs` with 2 orgs visible (`kiki-test-007` w/ Anrufe 5 / KVAs 2 / MA 4 / Termine 11, plus `kiki-customer-009` Wilhelm Selting w/ Anrufe 1) and no error block. - **2026-05-26:** **KVA `sent_at` stamp fix (follow-up to P0.5 side-finding).** `backend/app/api/routes/cost_estimates.py::set_status` was building its stamp map inline as `{"accepted": "accepted_at", "rejected": "rejected_at"}.get(payload.status)` — missing `"sent": "sent_at"`. So any PATCH to `/api/cost-estimates/{id}/status` with `status="sent"` would update only `status` and leave `sent_at` NULL, which silently kills the AI Insights `kva_followup` suggestion (the `_ai_insights` defensive `if sent` guard skips NULL-`sent_at` rows). `CostEstimateStatus` schema docstring explicitly lists `sent` as a valid status, so the bug was reachable even though no current frontend caller hits it (frontend only sends `'accepted'`; the `POST /send` route still correctly stamps `sent_at`). Fix lifts the stamp map to module scope as `_STAMP = {"sent": "sent_at", "accepted": "accepted_at", "rejected": "rejected_at"}`, mirroring `invoices._STAMP`. 4 new tests in `backend/tests/test_cost_estimate_status_stamp.py` (sent stamps sent_at · accepted stamps accepted_at + no cross-stamp · rejected stamps rejected_at · draft/invoiced stamp nothing). Full backend suite: `35 passed in 59s`. **Existing row KVA-2026-00001** (`id=6a6e394a-939a-41d5-8e0b-606ae96c5405`, test org) is almost certainly seeded/manual-SQL data (no reachable frontend path produces this state); backfill `update cost_estimates set sent_at = updated_at where id = '6a6e394a-939a-41d5-8e0b-606ae96c5405' and sent_at is null` is **queued for Amber** to authorise + run via Supabase MCP. Commit `42fa6fa`.

## Deployment (Railway)
Both services live in the `kikijarvis-backend` project (env `production`):
- **Frontend** — service `frontend` → **https://frontend-production-4bdf.up.railway.app** (multi-stage `frontend/Dockerfile` → `serve -s dist` on `$PORT`). `VITE_API_URL` is baked at **build time** (Dockerfile ARG default) to the backend URL. Build root must be `/frontend`: deploy with `railway up frontend --path-as-root --service frontend`, or set the service's Root Directory to `/frontend` in the dashboard so plain `railway up` works.
- **Backend** — service `backend` → **https://backend-production-3f88a.up.railway.app** (`backend/Dockerfile`, gunicorn+uvicorn, Root Directory `/backend`). `CORS_ORIGINS` env must include the frontend origin.

**⚠ If the BACKEND URL changes, update every place that hardcodes it:**
1. ElevenLabs `hk_*` tool webhook URLs — re-run `scripts/create_hk_tools_safe.py <NEW_BASE_URL>`.
2. n8n → backend **post-call webhook** target.
3. ElevenLabs **Conversation Initiation Data Webhook Override** URL.
4. Frontend `VITE_API_URL` (Dockerfile ARG default) — rebuild + redeploy the frontend.
5. Backend `CORS_ORIGINS` (only if the frontend domain also changed).

**Changing the FRONTEND URL is easy** — nothing external points at it; just update the backend's `CORS_ORIGINS` to the new origin. To give it a friendlier name: either a custom Railway subdomain (e.g. `heykiki-crm.up.railway.app` — free, via the dashboard if the name is available) or a real custom domain like `app.heykiki.de` (own the domain + add the DNS CNAME Railway provides).

- **HEAD (main):** Kiki-Zentrale complete (this commit) — `feat: Kiki-Zentrale — full agent control with safety layer, snapshots, rollback, and audit`. Prior: `eb972ae` (docs: session handover).

  - Shell + Auth (Supabase email/pw + magic link, protected routes)

  - Anrufe / Call Logs (3-pane, Realtime, audio-on-demand)
  - Kunden (list + detail, documents, inquiries)
  - Kalender (FullCalendar + Geschäftszeiten + Projekt-Timeline toggle)
  - Mitarbeiter (employees, absences, invites)
  - Planungstafel (drag-drop assets, Gantt)
  - Kostenvoranschläge / KVA (fpdf2 PDF, live preview)
  - Katalog & Vorlagen
  - **Rechnungen / Invoices** (migration 0012) — list/form/PDF, KVA→invoice
  - **Projekte** (migration 0013) — list/form/workspace (9 tabs) + Calendar timeline
  - **Einstellungen / Settings** (migration 0014) — `/settings/:section` + personal modal
  - **Kiki-Zentrale** (migration 0015) — `/kiki-zentrale/:section`, 13 sections (Verhalten, Prompt-Editor, Pflichtfelder, Branche & Kontext, Terminregeln, Terminkategorien, KVA-Automatisierung, Preisauskunft, Leistungsangebot, Notdienst, Telefon, Ausgehende Anrufe, Verlauf & Rückgängig). Safety layer `services/elevenlabs_agent.py`: cross-org guard → pre-write snapshot → additive array merge → **audio assertion** → surgical PATCH → post-write verify → **auto-rollback** → per-field audit. 35 endpoints; 8 unit + 6 live tests green; E2E 15/15.
- **Remaining: none — all CRM modules complete.**

## 2. Tech stack
- **Frontend:** React + TS + Vite, Tailwind (CSS-var design tokens), TanStack Query, React Router, Radix UI, FullCalendar, @dnd-kit. **Local-only** (`localhost:5173`, not on Vercel yet).
- **Backend:** FastAPI on **Python 3.13** (venv `backend/.venv`), deployed to **Railway** (`railway up`, NOT the MCP plugin). Runs locally **without `--reload`**.
- **DB:** Supabase Postgres, project `ifbluvdcbcesuhvkxsfn`. Migrations 0001–0014, applied via Supabase **MCP `apply_migration`** (no CLI). RLS scoped by `org_id`; backend uses service role (bypasses RLS).
- **Voice:** ElevenLabs agents (Kiki) via webhooks/N8N. **PDFs:** fpdf2 + bundled DejaVu fonts.

## 4. Hard UX constraints (applied throughout — keep applying)
1. **Left sub-nav swaps content** — one section visible at a time, no endless scroll.
2. **One primary green save button** visible at a time per section.
3. **German UI labels** throughout (code/comments English).
4. **Lucide icons only.**
5. **TanStack Query `staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000`** on all data fetches.
6. **Accent color as a CSS variable** (`lib/accent.ts applyAccent()` overrides `--green-*`) — never hardcode `#4a9b3f`.
7. **Deep-linkable sub-routes** (`/settings/{section}` pattern; `useParams`).
8. **Accordions start collapsed.**
9. **Action before diagnostic** (e.g. push: "Aktivieren" first, technical status collapsed below).
10. **No duplicated UI** between similar contexts (one shared component, e.g. placeholder chips for both invoice + KVA templates).

## 5. Kiki-Zentrale safety constraints (FRONT AND CENTER)
- **Additive provisioning only — never overwrite.** Do NOT replace `system_prompt` / `prompt`, `first_message`, or `client_events`. Merge/append; preserve existing values.
- **`client_events` must always include `"audio"`** — write the FULL required set, never a subset that drops audio (breaks call audio capture).
- **Duplicate-check on every write** — read current config first; only add what's missing (mirror `scripts/create_hk_tools_safe.py` idempotent pattern).
- **Read agent config via direct ElevenLabs API curl** — the Supabase/other MCP does NOT expose agent `tools`/`client_events`. Use:
  `curl -H "xi-api-key: $ELEVENLABS_API_KEY" https://api.elevenlabs.io/v1/convai/agents/<SAFE_AGENT_ID>` (`ELEVENLABS_API_KEY` is in `backend/.env`).
- **Never reference the production agent** `agent_7201…` in code, env, scripts, or API calls. Operate only on the safe agent / the test org's stored agent id.

## 8. Known pitfalls (do not repeat)
- **Preview screenshots are stale/downscaled** → trust `preview_eval` DOM reads as authoritative.
- **Radix menus/dialogs don't open via synthetic `.click()`** → dispatch `pointerdown`+`pointerup`+`click`; set React-controlled inputs via the native value setter + `input` event.
- **Backend has no `--reload`** → restart uvicorn after backend edits or routes go stale (405).
- **Supabase MCP `execute_sql` returns only the LAST statement's result** for multi-statement queries — query one thing at a time.
- **`public.users` vs `auth.users` name collision** — schema-qualify (`public.users`) in migrations.
- **Route module name vs config object:** `app/api/routes/settings.py` collides with the `settings` config object → import aliased (`settings as settings_routes`) in `main.py`. Same trap likely for a `kiki`/`agent` module — check.
- **Encrypted-field pattern** (`email_configs`/`pds_configs`): store `*_encrypted`, **never return ciphertext** (return `has_password`/`has_api_key` booleans), and **only re-encrypt when a new secret is supplied** (empty input = keep existing). Reuse `app/core/crypto.py` (`encrypt`/`decrypt`).
- **Address JSONB:** PATCH replaces the column **wholesale** to drop legacy `{raw}` — don't merge old + new keys.
- **Migrations:** write the `supabase/migrations/00XX_*.sql` file AND apply via MCP `apply_migration` (both).
- **Reference-product UX we deliberately diverged from:** no infinite settings scroll (sub-nav), no nested horizontal tabs (radio-cards), no duplicated placeholder UI, action-before-diagnostic, 2×2 grids for 4 peer items.
